<rate>4<//rate>< Review>
Great little trainer on the outskirts of Palm Springs. Small and intimate with a couple of belay walls and a couple of bouldering walls with standard terrain options and true-to-outdoor route grades. Great sets with challenging ratings, classes for all ages. Be aware - no locker rooms or showers available at this gym, so plan accordingly. Above all else - awesome staff and friendly community here, the two things that make any gym a pleasure to climb in. I'll definitely be visiting again!<//Review>

We went as a family with 13 year old son. Visiting his father for the summer we figured this would be a great way to spend time together, learn something new and build strength as a family and as individuals.

< Review>
I visited a couple months ago when I was in the area. Since it was off season, on a Friday afternoon, I was one of only two climbers, which was nice. The space is small, but good for training. They offer bouldering, ropes walls, and auto belay in a smaller room. The problems were definitely set with the area in Mind, because the grading is slightly harder than most indoor gyms. I'm not a serious climber, but was still able to find problems to climb.

Jesse, the manager, and another staff member were both incredibly welcoming and helpful. I imagine this is a great community based on the people. Glad I stopped in.<//Review>

<name>Dennis C</name>< Text>
Edit: Pizza buffet is from 11-2pm Mon-Fri!

Had the pizza buffet on 07/29/19 - will update this review once I try it again in a month or so. Since it was their first day open with the buffet there is obviously some room for improvement (credit card machine, pizza overcooked, etc), but the second batch of pizzas that came out were good. Breadsticks were also crunchy and dry and that didn't need to get replenished, so not sure if that was a one time thing. As it is new, very clean, nice staff, and a decent amount of sitting space. Will be interesting when/if this place gets more packed during the buffet times as there is probably only space for about four pizzas or so at a time.

I will be back!</Text>

< Review>
We have been when Fire Mountain Vet for two years now and in the 16 years that I've had a companion animal, they have been the most thorough and loving veterinary clinic we have ever trusted with the care of our two dogs. Dr. Vasilas and her staff take the time to get to know your companion, and your concerns. We recently had to say goodbye to our loving shih tzu at age 16 years and 9 months, and even in the midst of discomfort and confusion, he was wagging his tail when he saw members of the Fire Mountain team come in. The day we said goodbye was the most difficult in my life, and this team not only cared for our animals and assured that our shih tzu left this world peacefully, but they cared for us, the devastated pet parents,  and made everything as easy as possible for us in this process. I wish we had known this clinic from day one of pet parenthood.</Review>

<Review>I brought my 7 month old puppy here to be spayed after I cancelled my appointment at another vet here in town. I called on the evening of the 14th to see what their availability was after inquiring on their prices and reading their great reviews. The girl who answered the phone was extremely kind and helpful. I was expecting to wait at least a week or two to get my puppy in but was delighted when she said I could bring her in the next day! I brought her in, and unlike the previous vet,  the girl at the front seemed excited to see my puppy and myself and was very sweet. I had many choices I could add on with the surgery and found they were reasonably priced. I chose to have the laser add on and feel that it was a great decision. We have brought our dog to see Dr. Vasilas at Fire Mountain for the past 2.5 years. Although I live in La Jolla, the care at Fire Mountain is wonderful and is well worth the drive. < Text>
My 90 year old mother-in-law lives in Carlsbad and had not had any good experiences with the Animal Hospital in Carlsbad. She is elderly with an older cat and wanted a vet she could trust "not to take her to the cleaners" and give her cat good care at a fair price. I only come into town once or twice a year and when she asked me to "find a good vet", I felt fairly lost.

I am so glad we tried Fire Mountain. Dr. Cramer understood her concerns, her budget constraints and her wishes and gave Kissy the best care! The staff was very informative and helpful. The office and exam rooms were clean (they even smelled good!), and he listened to what she wanted before starting in on treatment she didn't want or need. The cost was extremely reasonable and I found everyone in the practice to be very professional. They even followed up by sending her a business card so she would have the information handy if she should need it.

Since I am away most of the time, I feel very confident that she will get the best care there ( and NOT be taken advantage of) if she should need to take Kissy in again. Having a vet I can trust is very important to me and I am relieved to know they are there when I can't be.<//Text>

< review>
We found Fire Mountain Vet Hospital by googling teeth cleaning for dogs. We had recently rescued a 3 year old Aussie named Newman who was in poor health, underweight, matted with lots of fleas. We made an appt right away with our prior Vet (who we love dearly) for a check up, shots and scheduled him to be neutered and discussed the fact that his teeth were in need of a cleaning badly. Three months later we take Newman in for the preop for teeth cleaning surgery and lab work. The bill for the lab work was $286.00 and the estimate from the 3rd party teeth cleaning was $550.00 to $857.00. I was not going to be gouged for teeth cleaning like so many people have been from the horror story reviews I read.

At this point my guard is WAY up after reading a plethora of reviews when I decide to call Fire Mtn Vet Hospital. The Vet Tech I spoke to told me their price of $199.00 (includes lab work) for a dog weighing over 35l bs.

To put this into perspective I'm an honest professional car salesman by trade, (yes this is possible) I deal with customers every day who have had a prior negative experience buying a car and they're waiting, looking for a lie to validate their fears from the past. In that moment I felt like the sweet little naive lady from Pasadena who had just met the most notorious evil slippery used car salesman stereotype. She's just been widowed having never made a vehicle purchase because her late husband always took care of that.
I was looking for the lie or up sale as this price was too good to be true. Upon arrival I hesitantly signed a waiver stating if while Newman was under anaesthetics and they found a tooth that needed to be pulled there would be an additional charge. Dr Krammer took the time to explain the procedure and the likely outcome. He was so thoughtful to us and to Newman, this man really loves dogs and appreciates his clients. An hour later we get a call from the Vet Tech, Newman did great and will be ready in 30 min she said. My first question was how much is the bill? Vet Tech replied $199.00. When we picked up Newman we brought our 13 yr old Standard Poodle (Zeke) with us who was due for an exam. Dr Krammer said he had time and saved us a trip back. I didn't ask price this time as Dr Krammer and his staff had earned our trust in every way a Vet should.

We now order our Royal Canin food through Fire Mtn as they are $8.00 less for a 24 lb bag and they match or beat pet meds for prescriptions. I didn't intend on writing a novel but I really wanted to give a shout out to all the great staff at Fire Mountain Vet Hospital, they're the best!!!

Randy, Lori, Zeke, Newman, Mr Boo, Purrla and Sox :)</review>

<text>This is such an awesome place just because it's a hut in the middle of a parking lot with plenty of shaded seating. It's also pretty cheap food for decent cheap Chinese food. They even take credit card!

<username>Star Traveler<//username>< Review>
It's fair to say that this place is a 'good deal' if you relate the quantity of food to the price.  However, I find the food here bland and without character, largely because of inadequate seasoning.  Also notable is that they use exclusively American vegetables (corn, mushrooms, carrots, green pepper, celery, broccoli) that are nearly the same in every dish.  You will not find any Chinese vegetables like water chestnuts, bok choy, bamboo shoots, bean sprouts, etc. being used here.  The result is rather unimpressive Chinese food that is not really Chinese food!< /Review>

< text>
I would call this place a hole in the wall, but that wouldn't be entirely accurate. It's more like hole in the street--you can see it from afar, but you don't pay much mind to it and instinctively avoid it. There isn't much signage, and it is very unassuming in that old donut shop way.

That however has no bearing on the type of food that comes out of here, however. The tastiest egg rolls (and large, too), the most flavorful Mongolian beef, and the kung Pao chicken exist here. Definitely something to check out.<//text>

< text>
My mom and I go here for late night nachos!

Super tasty.

We get the chicken nachos, lots of melted cheese, though, not as much as I would want, lots of grilled chunky chicken, lots of veg, a few slices of avocado, fresh tomato salsa, pickled veg. And nicely crisp tortilla chips. mmmmmmmmmmmm

Last night Mom had a particularly long day at work, so we were kind of tired and loopy. I'm just over a cold.

We walk in and there is a smartly dressed man at the register, Rick. He greeted us as we walked in, and we got to chatting about so much randomness. Nachos, horchata, and an in depth conversation about veganism and cow tounge... yeah, that was a weird turn... he had a bag he brought to my mom at the salsa bar, put the salsas we selected into the bag for us as we started heading out.

Dude was nice.

Hell, each time we come here the staff is friendly.

And the nachos are tasty. I really should try some other stuff, pics of the chiliquillies look really yummy. And signs say $1 street tacos on Tuesday.</text>

<userid>101746310625670370069<//userid><name>Russ Roberts< /name><Time>1581454268216</Time><Rate>4</Rate>< Review>
The supermarket has a nice mix of Asian items that cannot be found in the traditional Supermarket stores. Stores clean, the cashiers are polite, and the merchandise is nicely spaced. It's nice to see that it's not too crowded with trinkets and other low value items for no apparent reason compared to some other Asian markets. The only reason this gets four stars, is because some selections of the fresh produce that are usually present, may not be available. This may be of no fault to them, it may be strictly a seasonal thing. Perhaps there's not enough buying power from the small-market to be economically feasible.<//Review>
